When we crossed the ferry, almost all the cars were Gui ABC. We ate seafood noodles, Wenchang chicken, coconut juice, and drove along the coastal highway. The blue sky and clear sea waterğŸŒŠ made us feel good all the way.
At night, of course, the first choice is the Boao State Guesthouse, which is located in a Feng Shui treasure land. The hotel is built on the foothills of the main peak of Boao Longtanling, next to the permanent venue of the Boao Forum for Asia. It is a hotel where the central leaders receive dignitaries from various countries and take into account daily high-standard receptions.
As soon as we arrived at the hotel, we received enthusiastic service from the staff. We are very grateful to the manager for upgrading our family to a suite that usually sells for more than 3,000 yuan, and giving us two more breakfasts. The flattered joy came too suddenlyğŸ˜. Needless to say, the interior decoration and supporting facilities of the room are very complete and elegant. The 150-square-meter suite with two living rooms, two bedrooms and two and a half bathrooms is as comfortable as at home. Itâ€™s so good to live! Before going to bed, the waiter also brought Tremella soup and fruit, which is so thoughtful! The surrounding environment was very quiet at night, and the air conditioning temperature was just right, so I had a good night's sleep. In the morning, I woke up lazily to the chirping of birds and cicadas, and had a bowl of Hainan soup noodles, Qingbuliang, etc. among the various delicacies in the restaurant. It was another energetic and refreshing day!
I want to say that when traveling to Hainan, the Boao State Guesthouse is the first choice! Looking forward to seeing you next time!

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:6 Business Room - Garden-View (Double bed)
info:Stayed in January 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:15 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 12, 2023
msg:Boao State Guest House, a myth in Boao, has not lost its momentum after more than ten years, which is already very rare. The overall design style of the hotel has many similarities with the big tent of the iconic scenic spot in Boao, but the overall courtyard has a bright a**osphere of Hawaii and an international vision. It is said that dozens of heads of state attended the Boao Forum for Asia. place.
Although the hotel is divided into multiple areas, there is only one lobby. Therefore, no matter how ordinary a guest is, when he walks into the lobby, he will immediately feel intoxicated and satisfied like a state guest. The service personnel also provide high-standard service with the etiquette of state guests. Originally, I just booked the most ordinary Building 6 with the idea of trying it out, but Xiao Wang at the front desk offered to help me upgrade to Building 5, but I had the opportunity to appreciate the exquisite and high-end beauty of this hotel in detail. Thank you Xiao Wang!
Sure enough, the rooms in Building 5 are better than those in Building 6. It not only conveys the magnificence and dignity we felt when we checked in, but also the considerate service, as well as the intoxicating essence of Hainan traditional culture, and Comfortable and natural modern luxury design. I can see the designer's contemporary understanding and interpretation of Hainan's traditional culture, and every bit of respect for the local culture is extremely precious, which also fully demonstrates the hotel's sincerity in integrating into the local culture.
Only after looking at the magazines in the room did I know that the State Guest House was not joined by a well-known but seriously homogeneous international group hotel, but China's largest tourism central enterprise - China Travel Service Group. Only our own hotel companies in China, and only the Chinese hotel people who have been rooted in this land from toddler to gray-haired with the annual rings of the times, can accurately grasp that the State Guest House can meet the needs of the heads of state of various countries and demonstrate the fashion design concept , and the "degree" between the replica of local traditional culture, so that pure Chinese residents are fresh and will not have a sense of cultural difference.
Therefore, although I only lived in the hotel for one day, the experience was exceptionally good. Even if the 56-square-meter room is divided into several areas, it is not narrow at all, but the room insists on using a fully open design. It is full of sunlight, blank everywhere, tranquil and refreshing, pure and light, and simple. A big bed by the window can take a panoramic view of the lush green scenery. You don't need to open the window, and the lively and fragrant paintings are all in your heart. In the early morning, sitting on the balcony, looking at the hot springs and swimming pool at your feet, savoring the familiar aroma of bread, milk and fried eggs, and then flipping through the exquisite China Travel Magazine in the morning light, breakfast becomes the perfect way to enjoy the leisurely good time in the hotel. Great opportunity, intoxicated and amazing, Boao State Guesthouse is as beautiful as a fairyland!
